class=\"Date\"><span class=\"Prefix\">Updated on </span>May 16, 2021</div>\n      <div class=\"Description\">\n        <p>One Piece is an ongoing anime series that started in 1999. So far 977 episodes of One Piece have been aired. With a total of 95 reported filler episodes, One Piece has a very low filler percentage of 10%.</p>        <div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\" property=\"content:encoded\"><p>One Piece is the story of Monkey D. Luffy who became a rubber man after accidently eating a Devil Fruit. In his quest, Luffy builds his crew and continues on his adventure to find the mysterious treasure One
